          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;

        }

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>

        <p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





After enable the BluetoothRevamp feature, |BluetoothPrefStateObserver| will register a scoped observation |session_observation_|[1] to observe SessionManager.



<span class="line"><!---->After enable the BluetoothRevamp feature, |BluetoothPrefStateObserver| will register a scoped observation |session_observation_|[1] to observe SessionManager.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





And |session_observation_| only will be reset after the profile of primary users got loaded[2]. So if the user is not logged in or the logged-in user is not a primary user, |session_observation_| will not be reset.



<span class="line"><!---->And |session_observation_| only will be reset after the profile of primary users got loaded[2]. So if the user is not logged in or the logged-in user is not a primary user, |session_observation_| will not be reset.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





During BrowserMainRunner shutdown, |bluetooth_pref_state_observer_|[3] will be destroyed after |session_manager_| get reset[4]. Then, when the |bluetooth_pref_state_observer_| is being destroyed, calling RemoveObserver will trigger the UAF.



<span class="line"><!---->During BrowserMainRunner shutdown, |bluetooth_pref_state_observer_|[3] will be destroyed after |session_manager_| get reset[4]. Then, when the |bluetooth_pref_state_observer_| is being destroyed, calling RemoveObserver will trigger the UAF.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ash/net/bluetooth_pref_state_observer.cc;l=20;drc=50b7f4cf3ea84f170ee49c96b89617c2f8a4e59e"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ash/net/bluetooth_pref_state_observer.cc;l=20;drc=50b7f4cf3ea84f170ee49c96b89617c2f8a4e59e<!----></a>



<br>





[2]. 



<span class="line"><!---->[2]. <!----></span>

<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ash/net/bluetooth_pref_state_observer.cc;l=42;drc=50b7f4cf3ea84f170ee49c96b89617c2f8a4e59e"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:chrome/browser/ash/net/bluetooth_pref_state_observer.cc;l=42;drc=50b7f4cf3ea84f170ee49c96b89617c2f8a4e59e<!----></a>

<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>

$ ./out/x64_os/chrome --user-data-dir="/tmp/tt" --enable-features=BluetoothRevamp --login-manager



<span class="line"><!---->$ ./out/x64_os/chrome --user-data-dir="/tmp/tt" --enable-features=BluetoothRevamp --login-manager<!----></span>

then close browser.



<span class="line"><!---->then close browser.<!----></span>

[CrOS Bluetooth] Fix UAF in BluetoothPrefStateObserver.



<span class="line"><!---->[CrOS Bluetooth] Fix UAF in BluetoothPrefStateObserver.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Fix use-after-free caused by BluetoothPrefStateObserver when it is



<span class="line"><!---->Fix use-after-free caused by BluetoothPrefStateObserver when it is<!----></span>



<br>





destroyed in ChromeBrowserMainPartsAsh. Because it has an observer



<span class="line"><!---->destroyed in ChromeBrowserMainPartsAsh. Because it has an observer<!----></span>



<br>





to SessionManager, which is destroyed before BluetoothPrefStateObserver,



<span class="line"><!---->to SessionManager, which is destroyed before BluetoothPrefStateObserver,<!----></span>



<br>





when BluetoothPrefStateObserver is destroyed, it attempts to remove its



<span class="line"><!---->when BluetoothPrefStateObserver is destroyed, it attempts to remove its<!----></span>



<br>





observer to SessionManager which has already been freed, causing



<span class="line"><!---->observer to SessionManager which has already been freed, causing<!----></span>



<br>





a crash. This CL updates ChromeBrowserMainPartsAsh to reset



<span class="line"><!---->a crash. This CL updates ChromeBrowserMainPartsAsh to reset<!----></span>



<br>





BluetoothPrefStateObserver before SessionManager is reset, similar to



<span class="line"><!---->BluetoothPrefStateObserver before SessionManager is reset, similar to<!----></span>



<br>





what NetworkPrefStateObserver does.



<span class="line"><!---->what NetworkPrefStateObserver does.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<a class="strike-through" target="_blank" href="/p/chromium/issues/detail?id=1274061" title="Security: UAF in BluetoothPrefStateObserver"><!---->Bug: 1274061<!----></a>

[CrOS Bluetooth] Fix UAF in BluetoothPrefStateObserver.



<span class="line"><!---->[CrOS Bluetooth] Fix UAF in BluetoothPrefStateObserver.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Fix use-after-free caused by BluetoothPrefStateObserver when it is



<span class="line"><!---->Fix use-after-free caused by BluetoothPrefStateObserver when it is<!----></span>



<br>





destroyed in ChromeBrowserMainPartsAsh. Because it has an observer



<span class="line"><!---->destroyed in ChromeBrowserMainPartsAsh. Because it has an observer<!----></span>



<br>





to SessionManager, which is destroyed before BluetoothPrefStateObserver,



<span class="line"><!---->to SessionManager, which is destroyed before BluetoothPrefStateObserver,<!----></span>



<br>





when BluetoothPrefStateObserver is destroyed, it attempts to remove its



<span class="line"><!---->when BluetoothPrefStateObserver is destroyed, it attempts to remove its<!----></span>



<br>





observer to SessionManager which has already been freed, causing



<span class="line"><!---->observer to SessionManager which has already been freed, causing<!----></span>



<br>





a crash. This CL updates ChromeBrowserMainPartsAsh to reset



<span class="line"><!---->a crash. This CL updates ChromeBrowserMainPartsAsh to reset<!----></span>



<br>





BluetoothPrefStateObserver before SessionManager is reset, similar to



<span class="line"><!---->BluetoothPrefStateObserver before SessionManager is reset, similar to<!----></span>



<br>





what NetworkPrefStateObserver does.



<span class="line"><!---->what NetworkPrefStateObserver does.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<h3 class="medium-heading"><!----> issue</h3>


          


            

Target project:

<label for="targetProjectInput">Target project:</label>


            


              

<input id="targetProjectInput" aria-owns="chops-autocomplete-1" aria-autocomplete="both" aria-expanded="false" aria-haspopup="listbox" aria-activedescendant="">


              




      


        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }
